Local News

Shanghai Banking Community Cables US in Opposition to Raising Silver Prices 115

Also Requests the Ministry of Finance to Temporarily Suspend Approval of the Silver Agreement

Because Raising Silver Prices in the US Provides No Benefit to China

Recently, the US government, with the aim of raising silver prices, will be re-minting silver coins and has submitted it to the Senate for discussion. After this news was spread, the Chinese banking community believes that if this measure is implemented, China, as an import surplus country and a silver standard country, will inevitably suffer unimaginable consequences. Therefore, on the 20th of this month, in the name of the Shanghai Banking Association, representing all banks in Shanghai, a cable was sent to US President Roosevelt to express their views. At the same time, a cable was also sent to the Ministry of Finance, requesting the temporary suspension of the Silver Agreement produced at the World Economic Conference in order to cope with foreign currency aggression. However, within the banking community, due to the importance of this matter, strict secrecy was maintained to the outside world. After detailed investigation by a reporter from the East China News Agency, the details are recorded as follows:

Cable to the US President Expressing Opposition 116

Key figures in the banking community in this city believe that the US government's increase in silver prices will inevitably cause a large outflow of silver from China. After closely exchanging views, on the 20th of this month, in the name of the Shanghai Banking Association, representing all banks in Shanghai, a cable was sent to US President Roosevelt, requesting careful consideration. The original text was advisory in nature and not a protest. The wording did not explicitly oppose this policy of the US government, but in effect, it stated that the Chinese banking community, once this measure is implemented, expresses its utmost regret. According to a report from a reporter from the Shen Shi News Agency, the content of the cable was roughly as follows: (1) Explain China's current situation and economic conditions. (2) Based on China's current economic situation, the Chinese financial and business community will suffer serious losses as a result of the implementation of the US silver policy. (3) The sudden and high increase in silver prices in the US will cause irreparable chaos in China's international exchange rates. (4) It is hoped that the US government will implement the silver policy by gradually increasing silver prices, instead of taking sudden increases, in order to reduce the disorder of China's silver market. The above points are hoped to be noted by the US. After the cable was sent, according to news obtained by the banking community in this city, it is said that Roosevelt has agreed to consider it. However, he is currently unable to immediately indicate whether it is feasible.

Cable to the Ministry of Finance Requesting Delay of Approval of the Agreement 117

The banking community also sent a cable to Mr. Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance in Nanjing, on the same day, requesting a temporary suspension of the Silver Agreement produced at the World Economic Conference. This is because, at a time when the US government authorities are actively trying to increase silver prices, judging by their actions, it is inevitable. Although the banking community has sent a cable to the US President to state everything, there are fears that the effect will be minimal. At this time, the Silver Agreement is being sent to governments of various countries for approval. Once our government hastily approves it, it will be bound by this agreement for future silver issues and will not be able to operate freely. Therefore, it is specifically requested that the Ministry of Finance temporarily suspend approval of this agreement before the US government's silver price increase policy is fully understood.

Last Year's Outflow of Silver 118

According to the Bank of China's report yesterday, the amount of silver stored in this city is not large. According to yesterday's statistics, there are a total of 14,248,000 taels of silver, 33,678,000 yuan in silver dollars, and 15,819 large bars. Our country is a silver standard country, and most of the silver is concentrated in Shanghai. This report can prove the general situation of silver reserves in our country. According to Mr. Bei Songsun, in the past, silver mostly flowed into our country, but recently it is not the case. In 1929, the silver flowing into our country still reached tens of millions of ounces. However, based on last year's situation, the silver flowing from our country to foreign countries reached more than 50 million. Upon investigation, the cause of this trend is, of course, the alarming trade deficit, but the increase in overseas silver prices is also a factor. Now that the United States has raised silver prices, it is said that trade with China will increase compared to the past, which is very beneficial to China. However, this is just one side of the story from the United States.

Raising Silver Prices is Not Beneficial to Us 119

The banking community in our country stated that the rise in silver prices is a natural result of the rise in commodity prices, so this trend has no impact on society and international relations. Now, looking at the U.S. policy of raising silver prices, it only focuses on raising silver prices. This kind of expansionary policy is indeed beneficial to its dumping in China, but our country's goods will be affected by this and cannot be sold abroad. This situation will cause all the silver in our country to flow out, and what remains in the country will only be goods. The result will inevitably plunge our country's economic situation into a state of non-circulation and extreme chaos. If our country were a surplus country, the rise in silver prices would have no impact on us. But now it is not the case. The dumping of foreign goods year after year is becoming more and more intense. Even based on what was released yesterday by the International Trade Bureau, the trade deficit in January of this year has reached more than 40 million. Judging from this kind of statistics, it is even more clear that the increase in silver prices is harmful and not beneficial to us.

The North China Daily News Reports Luo Youfu's Telegram 120

The North China Daily News said that several Chinese bankers in this city telegraphed President Roosevelt, clearly stating that artificially raising the value of silver is not beneficial but harmful to China. It is heard that President Luo soon replied by telegram, saying that he would consider their opinions. The telegram was sent by a small group of bankers in a private capacity, so the text of the telegram was not made public. Zhang Gongquan, President of the Bank of China, Li Ming of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, and Bei Songsun, Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Bank of China, are all listed in the telegram. In addition, there are two other people. According to recent research, banker Mr. Xu once criticized the United States' wait-and-see attitude towards the use of silver as currency. The telegram sent this time is based on this idea, using clear words to oppose this kind of delaying attitude, and artificially raising the price of silver. The telegram stated that those who advocate this measure believe that it will be beneficial to China. It should be known that China is a country with a trade deficit, and artificially raising the price of silver will greatly hit China's welfare. It is heard that the central government is now closely watching the development of the U.S. silver problem. If the U.S. government decides to artificially raise the price of silver, the financial community in this city will implement corresponding remedial plans. However, when someone inquired about this matter from the authorities of the Ministry of Finance, they all remained silent. It is heard that the Ministry of Finance quite advocates the stability of silver prices. In the past two days, there have been rumors at home and abroad that the government is discussing suppressing the value of the national currency or prohibiting the export of silver, but according to a reliable telegram from Nanjing, the authorities have denied it.

Bei and Lin Express Their Opinions 121

A reporter from the China East News Agency visited Mr. Bei Songsun, Manager of the Shanghai Branch of the Bank of China, and Mr. Lin Kanghou, Secretary-General of the Banking Association, yesterday. According to Mr. Bei, the telegram to President Roosevelt, which was published in the North China Daily News, was sent by several of them in a private capacity, which is not accurate. Currently, Mr. Roosevelt has not yet replied to this. Regarding the U.S. government's policy of raising silver prices, some say that our country is a silver standard country, and that our purchasing power can be increased in the future, so it is considered beneficial. Some say that it will cause a large outflow of silver from our country, creating an economic panic. The latter observation is more thorough than the former. However, how will our country deal with this in the future? From a personal perspective, we still need to pay attention to the U.S. government's true attitude towards raising silver prices before we can determine anything. As for the saying that the export of silver should be prohibited, it can also be implemented when necessary, but there is no need for it at this time. According to Mr. Lin, in his personal opinion, this move by the U.S. government has a great impact on our country. In the past, the silver agreement concluded at the World Economic Conference is now being approved by the governments of various countries. In my opinion, implementation measures should be stipulated in the silver agreement, which may reduce international concerns about the silver problem. As for the prohibition of silver exports, this is indeed one of the methods, but the government authorities must also be fully prepared in advance to avoid difficulties. As for the telegram sent by the Banking Association to President Roosevelt, and the request to Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi on the same day to postpone the approval of the silver agreement, no reply has been received. As for the original text of the two telegrams, it is not yet possible to publish them due to their importance.

International Telegraph Office Conducts Trial Talk with England Last Night 122

The Results Are Quite Good and Trials Will Continue

Ownership of the Radio Station Has Been Accepted

After the Sino-British telecommunications began, the Ministry of Communications ordered the International Telegraph Office to prepare to hold mutual wireless telephone calls with European countries. It had held several trial talks with Britain and Germany. Last night, the office held another trial talk with England, and the results were quite good. The office is now preparing to implement long-term trial talks, scheduled for Tuesdays and Thursdays each week as the trial talk period. This trial talk is limited to within a few months, and when it is completely successful, it can be officially started. A reporter from the China East News Agency specially inquired about the trial talk situation yesterday, and the details are recorded as follows:

Trial Talk Last Night 123

Last night, the International Telegraph Office's sending and receiving department took advantage of the radio station to hold a trial talk with London, England. Here, the staff of the sending and receiving department were responsible, while the other party was the person in charge of the transportation agency under the jurisdiction of the highest postal and telecommunications authority in the United Kingdom. The two sides tested the sound for a long time, and the results were quite good.

Trial Period Specified 124

The International Telegraph Office has recently re-specified that this trial talk will be held every Tuesday and Thursday. The trial talk time is not fixed, because it can only be implemented after the radio station is free. According to the office, in order to be cautious, it is planned to hold long-term trial talks with European countries, with a period of several months. Currently, Britain and Germany have already achieved results in trial talks. After success, trial talks will be held one by one with the United States, France, Italy, and other countries.

Acceptance of Radio Station 125

In addition, the Sino-British radio stations for Sino-British telecommunications, which were recently held by the office, were all installed by the British Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company. Although the calls are now connected, the ownership and management rights of the radio station are still in the hands of the Marconi Company. The day before yesterday, the Ministry of Communications specially hired Zhu Qiqing, a commissioner from the National Defense Committee, to go to Shanghai to meet with Wen Yuqing, Director of the International Telegraph Office, engineers Zhang Chenghu, Shen Shuren, and technician Niu Yinliang, to accept the radio station project. They also held trials for the past two days and found that there were no drawbacks in the machinery. It is planned to report the trial process to the Ministry of Communications within a few days, and then the Ministry will pay the final payment to Marconi.

Most Are from the Northeast and Came to Shanghai from Peiping

The Yangtze River Rises and Navigation Resumes 127

Upstream and Downstream Ships from Today

Can Load Cargo and Pass Unimpeded

Since January 15 this year, the water level of the Yangtze River has been receding both upstream and downstream. Upstream, the Xindi had only five feet, blocking Jianglun for more than a month, and more than 30 ships were stranded and transshipped. Downstream of the Yangtze River, the water level at Madang first fell, and then Wuhu receded. At the shallowest time, it was only seven feet two inches, which is rare in the past 30 years. The grounding and blockage of upstream and downstream Jianglun, as well as the transshipment halfway, lasted for more than a month, with a total of about forty or fifty ships. The commercial and shipping industries suffered huge losses. It was not until yesterday that the wheel companies in this city received telegrams from Shashi Hankou stating that the water at Xindi had risen by two feet, and now reached seven feet. Shallow water Jianglun can be used for passage without having to be towed. Downstream, from Hankou to Jiujiang, the water is nine feet two inches, and from Jiujiang to Wuhu, it has risen to ten feet five inches. Yangtze River ships can load 50% of their cargo and are expected to pass without having to be transshipped. The ships that were grounded during the shallow water have all sailed out. From today, upstream and downstream wheels of the Yangtze River can come and go freely.

Sichuan River Wheel Alliance Increases Fees 133

Causing Sichuan Gang to Suspend the Handling of Goods

Increase of 100 Percent

Most of the Customs Brokers Disputed

The Sichuan River Wheel, the alliance cooperation, and the increase in the cost of water have been recorded in this newspaper. In recent days, the wheel company is still in a meeting on the issue of the size and weight of the grocery transport, and the Sichuan Gang Hakka, for this price increase, it is not possible to oppose it, but there are quite different opinions on the reform of the weight, etc. Yesterday, the Hakkas have telegraphed to Chongqing, please stop handling goods, in order to resist, the reporter will re-state the situation obtained from all aspects as follows:

New Rate Implemented 134

After the Taigu Yihua Minsheng Jiejang and others agreed on the Sichuan River Wheel Alliance and increased the cost of water, from yesterday, each wheel company has notified the customs brokers and the Hakkas to implement the new cost of water. Shanghai cotton yarn is transported to Chongqing, each piece increased from twelve yuan to twenty-two yuan, that is, from the Minheng wheel of Minsheng and the Gongping wheel of Jiejang to load export goods. The two wheels will go to Sichuan from Shanghai in the next two days, which is the first upstream ship after the Sichuan River Wheel Alliance and the increase in fees.

Second Price Increase 135

At the Jiejang meeting, the wheel companies originally agreed that after changing the two to yuan, even if the cotton yarn rose to 22 yuan, it would only be a little more than 15 taels. At a time when various consumption items in the shipping industry are increasing wildly, it is still impossible to make a profit. Therefore, after public discussion among the representatives of the companies, it is necessary to increase the Sichuan River movement by 100%. The 12 yuan cotton yarn is increased to 24 yuan, and other items such as pied head groceries and cigarettes are also increased by one fold according to the original cost of water. However, those that have already been announced are 10 yuan per piece of cotton yarn, etc. The remaining will be increased again from March 1st, and the new price of 100% will be charged.

Continued Discussion 136

There are many goods for which the price is increased, some are calculated by size, and some are calculated by weight. This time, the wheel companies publicly agreed that for the loading and transportation of each cargo, in addition to paying according to the newly set freight, the size and weight must be counted together with the bag skin box, etc., and there must be no so-called gross jin net jin discount as before. Those who occupy the area are also counted in this way, so yesterday afternoon, the representatives of the wheel companies gathered again in the Taigu company to discuss this issue.

Hakka Dispute 137

The Sichuan Gang customs brokers have a lot of disputes with the wheel company on the size and weight of the new agreed transportation of goods. The reason is that the gross and net calculation of the fee for the cargo, the measurement, all the Chinese wheel companies in the Yangtze River have always done so, and now once the new chapter is changed, it will cause a lot of losses to the loader. The company side, on the other hand, based on the foreign ship's fixed example, there is no way to charge the gross and net fee. This change in the cost of water is not specially created by the Sichuan River Wheel Bureau. On this issue, both sides have a lot of disputes, and it has not been resolved.

Suspend Handling of Goods 138

The Sichuan Gang Hakkas in Shanghai think that the cost of water that the wheel companies are discussing to increase now is too huge, and the original transportation rate is doubled. They are also so serious about the size and weight. The Hakkas have met many times, and they all think that there are still many stocks in Sichuan. Even if the current suspension of transportation, it will not have any impact on the Sichuan provincial market, and it can turn the price of goods slightly higher. Yesterday, the Sichuan Gang has publicly agreed and jointly telegraphed to Chongqing, reporting the situation of the Shanghai wheel companies increasing the cost of water, and please stop handling goods from today onwards, as the only way to deal with the Sichuan River wheel companies. The telegram was sent yesterday, and the goods going to the Sichuan River wheel will be greatly reduced.

The Shanghai-Peiping Train on Display Yesterday (Photo by Xu Tianzhang)

Car Body Appearance 143

Although the carriages of the train are made of wood and painted with blue paint, their appearance is no less beautiful than that of blue steel cars. All the signs outside the carriages are made of a bright metal, which is quite eye-catching. The organization of the entire train includes a first-class sleeper car with 16 berths, a first-class compartment sleeper car with 20 seats and 6 berths, two second-class sleeper cars with 30 berths each, a dining car, three third-class passenger cars with 94 seats each, and a heating and postal car, a luggage and conductor's car, totaling ten cars, accommodating 384 people.

Comfortable Facilities 144

The Shanghai-Ping Joint Transport Passenger Train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway travels a long distance and takes a considerable amount of time. To prevent passengers from becoming tired from their journey, the train is equipped with very comfortable facilities. These include the following features: (1) First-class sleeping cars, with eight compartments separated, each with two berths, one upper and one lower. During the day, the lower berth can be converted into a seat. In addition, the lounge car has three compartments with the same facilities. The lounge features extremely comfortable swivel chairs, which are especially popular with passengers. Each berth has a clothes hook and a storage net. If passengers have small items, they can be placed in the net to avoid loss. Second-class sleeping cars have seven compartments each, except for one with only one upper and one lower berth. The others have four berths each, and the upper berths can be folded up during the day to avoid interfering with seating. The berths are all made of leather and have springs inside, making them exceptionally soft. (2) In the dining car and sleeping cars, in addition to the usual large glass windows, there are small windows above that can be opened and closed at any time. Whether in winter or summer, there is ample fresh air. The ventilation is well-regulated, and the air contains very little smoke and dust, making it very suitable for travel hygiene. (3) All trains are equipped with heating. The sleeping car compartments also have heating regulators, which can be used to increase or decrease the temperature at any time. In summer, each compartment has a fan to avoid stuffiness. (4) Each berth is equipped with a lamp suitable for passengers to read books and newspapers. In addition to the electric stove and toilet, there are bright lights, making it convenient to enter and exit. There are also bright lights at the passenger entrances and exits of each car, not only preventing falls but also making it easy to identify the class of the car at night. The third-class cars have ten electric lights throughout, which are also quite bright. (5) In the first-class dining car, one part is the kitchen, and the other part is the dining room. The kitchen is equipped with a refrigerator, and the dining room has six large dining tables, each seating four people, and six small dining tables, each seating two people. In total, it can accommodate thirty-six people dining at the same time, and the space is quite spacious.

Scheduled Departure 145

Since the opening of the Capital Railway Ferry last October, the Shanghai-Ping Joint Transport service has been realized. Initially, the Beining Railway prepared one train, and the Jinpu Railway prepared five trains, forming trains No. 301 and 302, which ran every other day. The Beijing-Shanghai Railway should have prepared one train, but due to the lack of a lounge car, a dining car, and two second-class sleeping cars, its participation was temporarily delayed. The equipment was temporarily borrowed from the Jinpu Railway, and the Wusong Machinery Factory was urged to assemble the car bodies from the original undercarriages and rush to manufacture them. At the same time, the vehicles scheduled to be included were extensively repaired. Now that the work has been completed and the test run is good, it has been decided that Train No. 302, the third Shanghai-Ping through train, will begin running from Shanghai at 12:00 PM on the 25th of this month.

Construction Costs 146

Last night, Mo Heng, Director of the General Affairs Department of the Two Railways Administration, told a reporter from the Xin Xin News Agency that the Shanghai-Ping through train on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway has a total of ten cars, which were rebuilt by the Wusong Machinery Factory from the original undercarriages. The body renovation costs for the four cars, such as sleeping cars, lounge cars, and dining cars, totaled 177,000 yuan. Adding the costs of repairing other vehicles, the total cost was more than 200,000 yuan. It has now been decided to start running on the evening of the 25th, and the cars borrowed from the Jinpu Railway will be returned. The Railway Bureau also plans to have the Wusong Machinery Factory rebuild another train for its use.

American Aviator to Perform in China 147

Scheduled to Arrive in Port on the 12th of Next Month

Bringing a Large Airplane

According to the Hua Dong News Agency, since our country advocated aviation to save the nation, aviators from various countries have come to China to perform. Mr. Hawke, an American aviator, has also been invited by the United American Aircraft Company to come to China to demonstrate various aviation techniques. Mr. Hawke served in the U.S. Air Force for many years and participated in the European War. His long-distance flights have set special records. Invited by the United American Company, he left San Francisco on the President McKinley of the Dollar Steamship Lines the day before yesterday and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 12th of next month. According to Mr. Bao Lai, General Manager of the United American Company, Mr. Hawke is also bringing a Curtiss Condor large airplane. This aircraft can be used for transportation, passenger carrying, and bombing. For commercial use, it can carry 15 passengers, 450 pounds of luggage, and 200 pounds of mail, for a total load of 3,200 pounds. For military use, it can carry one 100-pound bomb, one 300-pound bomb, one 600-pound bomb, and one 1,100-pound bomb, for a total of four bombs. It can also be equipped with three active machine guns. Its average speed is 150 miles per hour, and its maximum speed can reach 170 miles per hour. In addition to the above load, it can also carry 600 gallons of gasoline. The aircraft is also being shipped to Shanghai on the same ship. After arriving in port, Mr. Hawke will fly the aircraft to demonstrate its techniques.

Finance Bureau Scheduled to Collect the 23rd Year Land Value Tax 148

The Deadline for Unpaid Taxes from Last Year is Extended by Two Months

The First Installment of This Year's Land Tax Will Be Collected Starting Next Month

The Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau announced that the first installment of the provisional land value tax for the 23rd year, which is due for collection in districts 1 to 7 of the Hunan area and districts 1 and 2 of the Zhabei area, is scheduled to be collected starting March 1st of this year. The deadline for payment is two months from the start of collection, ending on April 30th of this year. Landowners in the Hunan area should bring their receipts from the previous period and the notice for this period to the Municipal South Tax Collection Office of this Bureau at Maojia Lane in Nanshi for payment. Landowners in the Zhabei area should bring their receipts from the previous period and the notice for this period to the Municipal North Tax Collection Office of this Bureau at Datong Road in Zhabei for payment. Those who fail to pay within the deadline will be summoned and pursued for payment in accordance with Article 8 of the Provisional Land Value Tax Collection Regulations and Article 23 of the Implementation Rules, and annual interest will be charged on the amount owed, and the income from the land will be extracted and sold for compensation according to the number of years of arrears, in order to comply with the regulations and emphasize tax collection. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government and sending notices, this announcement is hereby issued to all owners to comply with and pay within the deadline without delay, lest they be punished. Furthermore, the notices sent by this Bureau do not incur any fees. If any owners have not received their notices, they should provide their current address or mailing address to this Bureau at Fenglin Bridge within the deadline for verification and resending. The deputy certificate can still be used to pay the tax along with the receipt from the previous period. Do not make a mistake. This announcement is issued on February 10th, 23rd year of the Republic of China, by Cai Zengji, Director of the Bureau.

Ma Heng's arrival in Shanghai will allow inventory to begin.

The Municipal Party Department's random inspection claim is completely inaccurate.

A Brief Account of the Tragic Disaster in Yuanwu County, Henan 158

The Chinese Jehol Relief Association recently reported that according to the Yuanwu County Party Department and various organizations in Henan, Yuanwu County is small, covering only about 30 square li. The soil is barren, and the people are poor. Even in good years, they are still in distress. In 1911 of the Republic of China, soldiers and bandits were frequent, and Yuanwu was in the direct path of conflict. In the past three years, it has suffered from successive droughts and floods, making the disaster even more severe. Last summer, locusts were rampant, destroying most of the autumn crops. Disasters occurred one after another. On August 9th last year, the River God raged, with water depths of more than seven feet on the flat ground and floods lasting for five days. South of the county seat, it became a swamp. Villages were destroyed, livestock were swept away, and crops were submerged. The losses were estimated at over 5 million yuan. Fertile fields were turned into silt, with dozens of li of barren land and no vegetation. 40,000 disaster victims have nowhere to live. Now, heavy snow has fallen, and there is solid ice on the ground. The victims have no clothes to cover their bodies and no grain to fill their stomachs. Tree bark and grass roots have been dug up and are almost exhausted. They have no way to beg, and they lack the resources to flee to other places. They are suffering from both cold and hunger, and people are dying on the roads. The tragic situation is difficult to describe. We implore you to quickly dispatch benevolent relief to Yuanwu to save tens of thousands of disaster victims from their precarious situation. The urgent telegram cannot express our anticipation and waiting for orders.

For several years, there has been no place in our country without disasters. The Yellow River has flooded, and the victims are in provinces such as Shandong, Henan, and Hebei. Tens of thousands of families are in distress. Conscientious people who read the newspaper can save their New Year's entertainment funds to help these surviving people. This is what we hope from compassionate comrades.

The Tea Industry Asks Anhui Province to Reduce the Business Tax 159

And Asks Not to Recruit Contractors

The Tea Association submits

Chen Zhaodao and others from the Shanghai Foreign Tea Association submit a document to the Ministry of Finance and the Anhui Provincial Government, stating the matter for which they are submitting:

Our export of boxed tea is suffering due to pressure from foreign teas, and sales have sharply declined, recently reaching almost zero. The government, to encourage exports, provides tax exemptions and tariff waivers. All miscellaneous taxes cannot be levied on exported boxed tea to protect domestic products and save tens of thousands of tea farmers, tea workers, and tea merchants. This benevolent policy has allowed us to continue operating. Last year, Anhui Province began levying a 0.4% business tax on boxed tea, which tea merchants painfully paid. This year, the tax has suddenly increased to 1.5%, which is like forcing a sick man to carry a heavy burden. How can we bear it? Furthermore, they are advertising for contractors, and the highest bidder wins, only knowing how to collect taxes and arbitrarily exploit us. According to the business tax regulations, a 0.2% tax is levied on tea, which includes domestic sales. It should be known that there are no taxes on exports from inland provinces, and heavy and light taxes should be handled separately. Regardless of whether the province's levy exceeds the scope, the tax levied last year cannot be increased this year. This principle is very clear. We implore you to telegraph the Anhui Finance Department, stating that the business tax on exported boxed tea should be handled according to the precedent set last year. Do not recruit contractors, as this would add another layer of exploitation. Payments can be made directly by the tea associations in each production area. We express our urgent plea and await your orders with utmost gratitude.

The Anhui Provincial Government replies

The Anhui Provincial Government's reply states:

The submission has been noted. The Finance Department is instructed to investigate and comply.

This reply.

Journalists' Association Discusses the Zhang Case 163

Believes the Nature of the Zhang Case Falls Within the Scope of Publishing Law

Notifies Members to Refrain from Further Comment

The Shanghai Journalists' Association, regarding the case of Zhang Jiping, editor-in-chief of the Shanghai Business News, who was sued for defamation for publishing news about the Ji-Xu lawsuit, had the Executive Committee decide to form a special committee, inviting legal experts to participate and conduct a legal study of the case. The special committee convened a meeting at the association's headquarters yesterday afternoon, which lasted until after 6 p.m. The members generally believed that the nature of the case, at most, fell within the scope of publishing law. It was decided that pending the final decision of the case, it was appropriate to wait for a fair judgment from the court. The association will also notify its members to attend the public hearing of the case at 2 p.m. on the 27th of this month in the First Tribunal of the Shanghai First Special District Court and to refrain from further comment.

Mayor Wu Hosts People from All Walks of Life to Raise Funds for the Leprosy Sanatorium 164

On-Site Donations Exceeded 10,000 Yuan, Approaching Success

The Site Has Been Surveyed in Wusong and Construction Will Begin Soon

The fundraising conference for the construction of the China Leprosy Sanatorium, initiated by the China Leprosy Relief Association, has achieved remarkable results after the active efforts of the association's General Secretary Wu Zhijian and Chief of Staff Zhu Shaoping. Wu Tiecheng, the Mayor of this city, strongly supports the project. To promote its early success and encourage the staff, he specially hosted people from all walks of life and team leaders and members at the Foreign Guests Reception Office of the Municipal Government on Xiafei Road at 4 p.m. yesterday to plan everything. The association's fundraising target was originally 100,000 yuan, and three-quarters had already been raised. Yesterday, Mayor Wu donated 5,000 yuan on the spot, and enthusiastic people from all walks of life donated more than 10,000 yuan on the spot. The remaining amount is less than one-tenth, and the project will soon be completed. The details are recorded below:

Attendance List 165

In addition to Mayor Wu, the leaders from all walks of life and the leaders and members of the fundraising teams who attended yesterday's gathering included Yu Qiaqing, Xu Xinliu (represented by Qiao Wenshou), Du Yuesheng (represented by Pang Jingzhou), Yan Fuqing, Xu Peihuang, Zhu Shaoping, Wang Xiaolai (represented by Li Dachao), Li Tingan, Yuan Ludeng, Xiao Zhiji's wife, Lin Huizhen, Lu Bohong, Chen Bingqian, Shen Yi, Lu Shaotang, Li Zushen, Lu Ganchen, Zheng Xitao, Tang Youwei, Xu Shuping, Yang Dunfu, Ding Fubao, Ding Huikang, Zhang Yishu, Hu Yongqi, Wu Yunzhai, Chen Liting, He Dekui, and more than forty foreigners.

Mayor's Speech 166

After the meeting began, Mayor Wu Tiecheng gave a speech, saying in essence that the purpose of inviting everyone today was to raise funds for the construction of the leprosy sanatorium initiated by the China Leprosy Relief Association. The fundraising work of the association began nearly five weeks ago, and it was inevitably somewhat delayed due to the Lunar New Year holiday. At present, only one-quarter of the target remains. With Shanghai's large population and your enthusiastic support, it will certainly not be difficult to achieve. The fundraising and preparatory work can be said to be already underway. I am willing to make a final effort to ensure its success. We must know that since we cannot live apart from society, we should naturally fulfill our unavoidable obligations in society. Moreover, this kind of undertaking seeks the welfare of society. Many foreigners have generously donated to this fundraising, which shows that the current concept of humanity towards society is different from the past and is gradually evolving from local to international. Chinese people are not inactive in relief and charitable undertakings, but most of them are close to passive methods, such as providing clothing and food only after people have suffered from cold and hunger. I hope that Chinese people will be aware of the need to adopt proactive methods in the future to prevent cold and hunger from occurring in the first place. The construction of the leprosy sanatorium is a proactive method of relieving society.

Yuan and Yan Give Speeches 167

Next, General Team Leader Yuan Ludeng gave a speech, saying in essence that he greatly hoped that the fundraising conference for the construction of the leprosy sanatorium by the Leprosy Relief Association would succeed. Half of the project has already been completed, and it is certain that it will be fully completed soon. He was very pleased. Leprosy is not easy to detect in cold climates, so it is not often found in Shanghai. He initially thought that only Guangdong and Fujian had the disease, but according to the reports and statistics from various hospitals in Shanghai, there are already more than 2,000 cases. Everyone does not pay much attention to it. If relief is not provided, it will become increasingly widespread in the future and will be unavoidable, truly becoming a great disaster. He sincerely hoped that those with the ability would bravely help. Then, Deputy General Team Leader Yan Fuqing, who is also the President of the China Leprosy Relief Association, gave a speech, saying in essence that leprosy relief efforts, whether indirect or direct, exist in many places, but they are limited by economic resources and cannot be expanded. The Philippine Department of Health's entire budget is 5 million pesos per year, and the amount used for leprosy relief accounts for 2 million pesos. Our country only spends 40,000 to 50,000 yuan per year, a vast difference. Therefore, he sincerely hoped that enthusiastic people from society could voluntarily support the development of this undertaking. Deputy General Team Leader Xu Xinliu then gave a speech on behalf of Gao Wenshou and Lu Bohong, which is omitted for brevity.

Work Report 168

The association's general secretary, Wu Zhijian, reported on recent progress, stating that fundraising efforts have reached three-quarters of the goal. The original date for the fourth and final announcement was February 10th, but it was temporarily suspended due to the lunar new year holiday. The deadline has now been extended to March 10th, which will be the closing date for fundraising. The total amount to be raised is 100,000, which will be used to start the construction project once collected. The site has been determined to be in Wusong Town, with over 100 acres of land purchased. Architect Fan Wenzhao has already created the drawings. The facilities of this type of leprosy sanatorium are different from the past. Previously, leprosy patients could only enter and not leave; entering the hospital was tantamount to dying. Now, with the advancement of science, a treatment for leprosy has been discovered. The purpose of patients entering the hospital is to be cured. The sanatorium also has workshops for patients to work in, hence the participation of the Vocational Education Society among the association's members. Each ward in the sanatorium will house a maximum of seven or eight, or five or six people. All facilities are exceptionally well-equipped. Construction is expected to begin soon.

Fundraising Conclusion 169

Subsequently, Secretary Gao Mingqiang reported the results of the fundraising. In addition to the 40,000 already secured, the results of the third phase of fundraising were announced on February 3rd. The actual amount received for the fourth phase of fundraising reached 5,275 yuan. Together with the previous three phases, the total is 15,426 yuan, 7 jiao, and 8 fen. The amount pledged is estimated at 18,665 yuan. The total of actual receipts and pledges reached 34,091 yuan, 7 jiao, and 8 fen. There were also on-the-spot pledges made today, including 5,000 yuan pledged by Mayor Wu, 3,000 yuan pledged by Chen Bingqian, 2,000 yuan pledged by Lu Bohong, 1,000 yuan pledged by Lu Shaotang, and 300 yuan pledged by Li Zushen, totaling 11,300 yuan. The shortfall is only over 9,000 yuan. However, many teams have yet to report their results, so it is expected that the goal will be reached soon.

Animal Protection Association Requests Strict Prohibition of Tortoise Killing 170

Shells Cracking, Flesh Dug Out, Fresh Blood Splattering

Heads and Feet Shrinking Tightly, Too Horrific to Witness

The China Animal Protection Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau yesterday, requesting that it issue orders to strictly prohibit the killing of tortoises in order to uphold benevolent governance and save sentient beings. The original letter is recorded below:

To the esteemed Bureau,

Previously, a letter from the Life Protection Newspaper, a member of our association, stated that along the riverbank in Xujiahui in this city, there are many small boats that specialize in catching and nailing tortoises year-round. The slaughter is even more severe during the autumn equinox. Every time they are slaughtered, shells are cracked, flesh is dug out, and fresh blood splatters. Heads and feet shrink into a ball, and they can still stretch out for a long time. If it were not for unbearable pain, why would they do so? Although tortoises are insignificant creatures, they are the longest-living animals, hence their difficulty in dying. At this time of autumn and winter, the intense heat will pass. Allowing blood and flesh to be scattered everywhere, attracting mosquitoes and flies, will further harm public health. This cruel behavior is heartbreaking to hear. Since these creatures do not harm humans and are not food items, why not let them live and die naturally? However, some ignorant people actually use this petty profit to abandon all conscience and resort to such cruel methods. Their cruelty is extreme. Therefore, we specifically request that your esteemed Bureau devise methods for relief to protect animals and other creatures.

In addition to replying to the letter, we hereby send this letter to your esteemed Bureau, requesting that you issue orders for strict prohibition to uphold benevolent governance and save sentient beings.

After investigation by the second team of detectives of the French Police, detectives Lu Zhulin and Wang Rusong, deputy detectives Zhang Daorong, and detectives Liu Jinrong, Shen Jinshi, and Lu Jinxiang, at 5 pm on the afternoon of the day before yesterday, bandits Xu Guifa (nickname Rotten Foot Ningbo or Foolish Da), Chen Rongsheng, Chen Jinchang, Chen Kejian, Chen Shurong, Zhang Qichang, Zhang Guibao, Zhang Asan, and female bandits Chen Ge, Chen Shi, and Huang Linmei, a total of eleven people, were arrested successively at No. 128 on Avenue Foch in the Public Concession and No. 18 Tianyou Lane, Haichang Road in Zhabei. During the postponement, it was found that the bandits had conspired to commit murder in October of the seventeenth year [of the Republic], and had robbed a bank of over 100,000 yuan four or five years ago. He requested another two weeks postponement to investigate the detailed facts of the case and sue for trial. Subsequently, the lawyers Wang Shizong and Li Pengcheng, hired by Chen Ge, Chen Shi, Zhang Asan and others, stated that the defendants had committed relatively minor crimes in the case and requested that they be allowed bail during the postponement, pending trial. The court verified the report, briefly questioned each defendant, and ordered that the case was serious, bail was not allowed, and the trial would be postponed to March 6th. The defendants were still sent back to custody separately.

Rugao Kidnappers Transferred 174

No Crimes Committed in Shanghai

Seven Bandits Allowed to Be Transferred to Water Police

Lu Zicai's beloved five-year-old son, Zhongbao, a resident of No. 41 Yingfeng Lane, 14th District, Rugao County, Jiangbei, and the head of the local district defense corps, was kidnapped at the end of the lunar third month of last year [of the Republic] and hidden away, demanding a huge ransom of 17,000 yuan. The bandit gang was captured by the 11th Detachment of the 3rd District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Corps stationed in the county and sent to the 3rd District for transfer to the Jiangsu Security Office for interrogation. At the beginning of this month, the victim, Lu Zicai, received another letter from the bandits, asking him to come to Shanghai on the 10th to negotiate the ransom in the Rue du Marché in the French Concession. Because Lu Zicai had difficulty raising a huge amount of money, he reported it to the 3rd District of the Water Police Corps, which sent personnel to come to Shanghai with him to report to the French Police for assistance in the arrest. The Special Organ Inspector, Jin Jiulin, along with Detective Zhang Ziying, Deputy Detective Zhou Bingcheng, and undercover detectives from the general shift, rushed to the corner of Rue du Marché and Avenue Birt on the morning of the incident to wait, and according to the kidnappers' agreement, ordered the victim's side to send someone with a white briefcase as a sign. Not long after waiting, kidnappers arrived to negotiate, and the bandits Shao Jinlan, Yan Changcai, Gong Zhihua, Yan Shoucai, Yang Shoufu, and others were arrested. In addition, the young hostage Lu Zhongbao was found in the back room of No. 5 Fude Lane, Minli Road, Zhabei, and the old woman watching the hostage, Wang Xu, and the young woman, Deng Xiayun, were also arrested and taken back to the police station for interrogation and detention by the Second Special District Court in order to investigate whether the bandits had committed other crimes in Shanghai. The postponement of the trial to the 26th has already been reported in the previous newspapers. The French Police have already found that the criminals had not committed any other crimes in Shanghai, so no public prosecution was filed. The Director of the 3rd District of the Jiangsu Provincial Water Police Corps stationed in Nantong, Chi Yaozhong, sent Detective Director Zhang Jingtang to Shanghai with a document, requesting the Second Special District Court to transfer the defendants to be tried. The court notified the police station, and at 10 am yesterday, seven male and female bandits and the hostage were escorted to the court. Judge Sun Penghang took the seat in the Second Criminal Court for interrogation. First, the police lawyer Yao Zhaodi stated that the defendants had committed a kidnapping case in Rugao County in the mainland, and negotiated the ransom in Shanghai. The French Police assisted in the arrest based on the report. Now it has been found that the defendants have not committed any other crimes in the concession. The police station has no objection to the Water Police Corps' request for transfer. Judge Sun verified the report, questioned the defendants, reviewed the Water Police Corps' document, and summoned Zhang Jingtang, the Detective Director of the Water Police Corps, to the court to inquire about the handling of the case. He then ordered that the seven defendants, along with the hostage, be handed over to Zhang Jingtang, the Detective Director of the 3rd District of the Water Police Corps, for trial in the case.

Male Corpse with Seven Knife Wounds in Xiaoche River, Yinxiang Port 175

Appears to be Gutted

The Murderer's Methods Are Too Cruel

A male corpse was found in the Xiaoche River at the end of Ningguo Road, Yinxiang Port, yesterday morning. Only the top of the head was exposed with knife wounds. Several steps away from the corpse, on the riverbank, there was a pool of blood and a felt hat was left behind. The local security guard noticed it and immediately reported it to the District Court for autopsy. Prosecutor Li Fen, accompanied by examiner Xuan Zhiming, arrived at the scene. The corpse was identified to be about twenty years old, wearing a blue cloth cotton robe, with a blue cloth cotton padded jacket inside, blue cloth leggings and cotton trousers, and a blue cloth short sports pants on the outside. The head had seven knife wounds, and the front chest had two knife wounds. It was observed that the murderer seemed to want to cut open the abdomen. It was confirmed that the death was due to knife wounds. The corpse identification form was filled out. Since no family members came to claim the body, it was ordered to be collected by the court for investigation and handling of the murderer.

Japanese Newspaper Reports Sharp Decline in Japanese Silk Sales 179

Inventory Reaches 50,000 Bales

According to the Japanese newspaper Mainichi Shimbun yesterday, since November of the lunar calendar last year, the cotton industry in this port has been in a slump, but everyone hopes for an improvement this spring. Unexpectedly, all places are still idle as before, without any sign of recovery. The inventory of Japanese silk at the end of January reached 30,000 bales, and the output of manufactured goods is also increasing day by day, so that there is no room for self-use warehouses. Judging from the current situation, it should be more than one million bales by the end of this month. Looking back at the market conditions of Japanese silk in January last year, although the Shanhaiguan and Rehe issues continued to occur, the transaction was still good until the end of the lunar new year. Therefore, compared with the same period last year, the sales volume is vastly different. Moreover, there have been no major unrest incidents at home and abroad this year, but the sales volume is contrary to the past, indicating the poverty of the economic sector and a sharp reduction in purchasing power. It is heard that from the end of January to the present, the accumulation of Chinese silk is also 135,000 bales, and each Chinese factory has suspended business due to the old New Year, when it is around 50,000 to 60,000 bales.

Navigation Administration Forbids Crew Members from Serving During the Certificate Application Period 192

China Association of Ship Engineers Submitted a Petition to the Ministry for Correction Yesterday

The China Association of Ship Engineers recently petitioned the Ministry of Transportation to stop the Shanghai Navigation Administration from forbidding crew members in the certificate application period from serving on ships. The original text read:

Submitting a petition for being denounced due to official business, making things difficult for no reason, petitioning for justice, strictly investigating and punishing to uphold the law and purify officialdom.

The association previously submitted a petition for the Shanghai Navigation Administration's handling of crew members impersonating others, serving without certificates, and illegally favoring them without taking action, resulting in the unemployment of most crew members with certificates. This petition was submitted to the Ministry for thorough investigation.

During this investigation period, the association believed that the facts were there, and no matter what, it would be difficult to deny them. In the future, the solution will be revealed. Unexpectedly, the bureau did not reflect on itself, but instead harbored resentment because of this, and used its power to destroy the association's members to vent its anger. Li Junjin, a member, has been working as a second engineer on the Yong'an ship of the Dazhen Company for a long time. In December of last year, he entrusted the association to apply for a Class B Second Engineer certificate on his behalf. Only because the ministry had not approved the petition for many days, he was waiting quietly for inspection and processing. On the 30th of last month, the bureau suddenly pointed out that he had not received the certificate, refused to close the customs, and did not handle it according to the established practice of allowing crew members to serve during the certificate application period. Although the association prepared a letter of proof for him, it refused to accept it. The member was forced to leave the ship and leave his job, suffering damage.

It is the bureau's duty to allow crew members to serve during the certificate application period. How can it pretend not to know? If it is said that the approval is not followed, it is not credible, then the time of processing is either slow or fast, which is not something that the association can ask. However, since it has prepared a letter of proof, if it is false, the person in charge is responsible. Why must it be demanded outside the law? If it is not for being denounced due to official business, and it is not hesitated to use accidents to seek revenge, disturb the association, it will not be so oppressed. With this phenomenon, the association believes that the gap has been opened, the future is long, and the future troubles are worrying. For this reason, a text is prepared to detail the details and send the original letter together. Please uphold justice, strictly investigate and punish, to uphold the law and purify officialdom. The association is fortunate, and the shipping industry is fortunate.

American Doctor Robert Sheng Narrowly Escapes Bandit Kidnapping 193

Bullet Pierces Coat Corner, Luckily Unharmed

Police Arrest Several Kidnappers

Robert Sheng, a Western doctor from the Bureau of Industry and Commerce, drove his own car, No. 6884, on the morning of January 31st, before dawn at around 3 am, intending to return to his residence. Unexpectedly, he encountered several bandits on Route Haddon in Western Shanghai. They jumped into the car and monitored Robert Sheng, driving straight to Route de la Gare in the French Concession. Because the Westerner shouted loudly, he was shot by the kidnappers as a warning. The bullet pierced through the corner of the Westerner's coat, luckily without injury. The bandits were also afraid of failure, so they got out of the car together and fled. Afterwards, the Westerner reported the case to the police station and asked for investigation. Since the occurrence of this case, the police stations have paid great attention to it, and all Chinese and Western detectives have been ordered to pay attention and investigate. The Chief Inspector of the Police Department, Lu Liankui, Detectives Shen Tianbao and Zhou Honglin, etc., learned that the bandits in this case were hiding at No. 1, Lane 23, Rue Birt in the French Concession. They secretly went there with weapons at around 6 am yesterday, along with Detectives Liu Shaokui and Feng Zhiming, etc. They arrested several male and female bandits at the address with the cooperation of French police detectives and took them back to the police station for interrogation. One of the bandits admitted to the kidnapping and confessed that there was a pistol and seven bullets hidden in the ditch near the Hongqiao Airport. The Chinese and Western detectives then went to the airport with the police detectives from the Sixth District Public Security Bureau, searched out the guns and bullets, and brought them back to the police station. The police station is now investigating the remaining fugitives in detail, so that they can be sent to the First Special District Court for trial in the coming days.

Dispatch to the Health Authorities of Beijing and Shanghai

Since the successive completion of the highways in five provinces and cities, great attention has been paid to safety equipment along the roads. Business Development of Great Wall Company 195

The phonograph record industry has long been dominated by foreign merchants. The Great Wall Company is the only one founded with purely Chinese capital. The shareholders of the company are all well-known figures in Shanghai, such as Zhang Xiaolin, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Danru, Li Zushen, Lai Yongfang, Sheng Zecheng, Yao Mulian, Wu Yunzhai, Li Gufan, Li Zuen, Wang Wenzhi, Qin Daishi, Yu Yefeng, Chen Bo, Sun Nong, and many other celebrities, as well as the late Li Huiwu and Wang Xinguan. All of these gentlemen are the founders of the company. Its financial strength is enough to make the various companies operated by foreign merchants look at it with apprehension. Since the company started business last year, it has released more than one hundred types of records. The quality of the selected songs and the number of invited performers have truly set a new record never seen before in the record industry. Among its unique and rare products are the "Si Wu Hua Dong" sung by the Four Great Dan Actresses, the complete "Farewell My Concubine" sung by Mei Lanfang and Yang Lou, Yu Shuyan's "Zhuo Fang Su Dian," "Zhai Chan Hui," "Shi Jie Ting," "Wu Long Yuan," Mei Lanfang and Jiang Miaoxiang's "Mu Tian Wang," Mei Lanfang and Ru Fuhui's "Nü Qi Jie," Cheng Yanqiu and Wang Shaolou's "Fen He Wan," Shang Xiaoyun and Wang Xiaolou's "Wu Jia Po," Meng Xiaodong's "Zhuo Fang Cao," "Zhu Lian Zhai," Yang Xiaolou and Hao Shouchang's "Lian Huan Tao," "Ye Zhu Lin," Wang Ruiqing and Cheng Jixian's complete "Yue Lai Dian," and Zhang Eyun's "Su San Qi Jie." All of these records are famous operas that have never been recorded before. Therefore, within a year of release, sales have reached over 200,000 copies. Such achievements can be considered good news for a domestic enterprise. It is also reported that the company plans to hold a third recording session in the autumn to strengthen its resources and intends to broadly record the famous performers who were previously missed.

Burglary by Prying Doors on North Fujian Road 196

Citizens' Association of the Road Sends Letter to the Police Station Requesting Investigation

The Fuhua Xiang Foreign Goods Store at No. 88 North Fujian Road in this city was broken into by burglars who pried open the front door late at night on the 21st. Twenty-five pieces of silk fabric, worth about three to four hundred yuan, were stolen. Afterwards, it was learned that, in addition to the store reporting to the local police station, the store is located in the center of the road, and the burglars dared to pry open the door and calmly commit the theft, which must have taken a long time. This indicates that the police protection is insufficient. Therefore, a letter has been sent to the 37th District Citizens' Association and the North Fujian Road Businessmen's Association, requesting them to forward it to the Police Department for investigation. The two associations sent a letter to the Municipal Council's Police Department yesterday, stating (excerpted above): "This road is short and convenient for transportation, connected to the Old Zha Gate Bridge in the south, and is a main thoroughfare for pedestrians. It is a place where patrols pass by and guards are stationed. The store is located not far from the local police station. How could the store be calmly burglarized without the detectives being aware of it? This makes all the stores in this area feel uneasy. Therefore, we earnestly request you to order your subordinates to quickly investigate and solve the case, and to increase patrols at night to protect the city and maintain the residents' safety. We extend our respects."

Total Amount of Silver Transported on Two Railways in the Second Half of Last Year 197

Totaling 57,200,000 Yuan

In the second half of last year, the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways transported a total of 23,135,500 yuan of silver from Shanghai to major stations along the Shanghai-Nanjing line. The amount transported from various stations to Shanghai totaled 24,135,900 yuan. The amount transported to major stations along the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line totaled 4,967,300 yuan. The amount transported from various stations to Shanghai was the same. The total for both railways was 57,200,600 yuan. The total amount for November and December was the highest. The total for November was 8,314,200 yuan, and the total for December was 14,317,000 yuan.

Railway Bureau and Asiatic Petroleum Company Agree to Install Gas Station at North Station 198

Fuel for the Railway Bureau Calculated at Special Preferential Rates

The Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus have never had gas station facilities for public motor vehicles. Recently, they negotiated preferential terms with the Asiatic Petroleum Company. The price of gasoline used by the bureau will be calculated at a special rate. Therefore, a Shell gasoline station with a capacity of 5,460 kilograms will be installed at the Shanghai North Station, specifically for refueling the bureau's motor vehicles. Employees of the bureau who own their own cars can also refuel at this station and pay at the actual price paid by the bureau. The General Affairs Department has consulted with the Traffic Department and drafted eight management rules, which have been approved for implementation. The rules are as follows: (1) The gasoline station established by the bureau at the Shanghai North Station will have one staff member assigned by the Affairs Department as the manager, and one servant will be assigned nearby to be in charge of the management, both of whom will be supervised and guided by the Affairs Section of the General Affairs Department. (2) When the bureau's public motor vehicles need fuel, the person in charge from the Affairs Section of the General Affairs Department will issue a fuel requisition form, which will be given to the driver, who will take it to the gas station to obtain fuel. (3) The manager should record the quantity, date, and other details of fuel received, dispensed, and stored in the account book issued by the Affairs Section of the General Affairs Department for verification. (4) The manager should record the total amount of fuel stored. (5) Every week, the Affairs Section of the General Affairs Department will send personnel to check and verify the quantity of fuel stored and dispensed with the manager to ensure that it matches the amount recorded in the book. If there is any discrepancy, the reason for the discrepancy should be immediately investigated and reported to the responsible officer for handling. (6) If an employee of the bureau owns a motor vehicle and wants to refuel at this station, the employee must obtain a certificate from the department in charge and obtain a fuel requisition book from the Affairs Section of the General Affairs Department. The user must sign the book to obtain fuel from the gas station. (7) When an employee of the bureau obtains a fuel requisition form from the Affairs Section of the General Affairs Department, they must leave a seal or signature sample for verification. (8) The gasoline used by an employee of the bureau at this station will be settled monthly. The user must pay the fuel cost to the Affairs Section of the General Affairs Department for transfer to the Accounting Department within five days after receiving the bill or notification. If the payment is overdue, the preferential benefits will be immediately terminated, and the Accounting Department will be notified to deduct the overdue payment from the user's salary.

Brief Biography of Xiao Weiguo, the New Director of the Traffic Department of the Two Railways 199

Xiao Weiguo, the new director of the Traffic Department of the Two Railways, took office on the 21st of this month. Mr. Xiao is 35 years old, from Pingxiang, Jiangxi Province. He graduated from Peiping Jiaotong University. From 1923 to 1926, he served as the chief stationmaster of freight transportation on the Jiaoji Railway. In 1927, he was appointed by the General Headquarters of the Revolutionary Army as a special commissioner for military and party affairs of the Zhilu Army. In 1928, he served as a staff member of the Road Administration Department of the Ministry of Communications and as an executive member of the Special Party Headquarters, a front-line transportation commissioner of the War Zone Political Affairs Committee, and director and acting director of the Traffic Department of the Jiaoji Railway. In 1929, he served as the director of construction of the Hunan Provincial Government. In 1930, he served as the director of the Railway Management Department of the Yang Northeast Transportation Vocational School, and as a professor of Railway Transportation, Railway Accounting, and Railway Vehicles. After the September 18th Incident, he served as the director of construction of the Shanxi Provincial Government and as a member of the Transportation Committee of the Provincial Government, a professor at Shanxi University, a staff member of the Ministry of Railways, and an official of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration. During his tenure as secretary of the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, he made many suggestions for all reforms. Especially in terms of traffic, there have been excellent achievements due to his suggestions and improvements. This time, he assumes the position of director of the Traffic Department, which will allow him to further display his talents.

The Reduced Rent Committee of Hankou Shanxi Second Road Actively Campaigns 206

Distributing Rent Survey Forms to Households in the District

The Hankou Shanxi Second Road Businessmen's Association Branch and the 21st District Citizens' Association Branch believe that since the January 28th Shanghai Incident, the city's prosperity has been declining, businesses have been withering, industries are struggling to maintain themselves, and citizens are becoming increasingly impoverished, which has a significant impact on social stability. The association, recognizing this, is committed to alleviating the suffering of citizens and reducing their burden. With this aim, the Reduced Rent Committee Branch of Hankou Shanxi Second Road was organized. In addition to reporting to the higher authorities for registration, they have specially prepared rent survey forms, which will be distributed to households in the district for completion and return to the association within three days for collation and statistics to facilitate further action. The form requests households to clearly state the name of the business, the name of the manager, the number of rooms rented, the monthly rent, whether there is a lease, whether the rent has been increased, the date of the rent increase, the year the building was built, the name of the landlord, and whether they are renting directly, so that the information can be registered and distributed.

Reading Questions and Answers

Reading Guidance:

Preliminary Reading of Social Sciences (Continued) 218

As for the subsequent research order, if you have the above foundation, you can develop in any direction you like, and you will have considerable expertise. If you are interested in politics, you can focus on studying modern politics, especially the various forms of dictatorship and autocracy currently popular, as well as the democracy of Europe and America in the past, etc. If you are enthusiastic about religion, you can study the nature of Christianity, or the function of Christianity? If you are fascinated by art, you can study literature, painting, sculpture, music, etc., by category.

This is one path.

As for which books are most suitable as reading material? This is naturally very difficult to say; and it also depends on the level of each reader. Now let's just list a few of the most basic books for readers to refer to.

A. According to the first research order, you can read:

"World History" translated by Shi Fuliang, Dajiang Edition

"Introduction to Social Sciences" written by Sugiyama Sakae, Kunlun Edition

"Fundamental Problems of Social Science in Theory and Practice" translated by Li Da, Kunlun Edition

"Social Science | Two Lectures" written by Sugiyama Sakae, Lehua Edition

Of the above three, you can choose to read one or two.

"The System of Economic Phenomena" written by Chen Baoyin, Lehua Edition

"Outline of Economic Science" translated by Shi Cuntong, Dajiang Edition

"Outline of Economics" translated by Chen Baoyin, Lequn Edition

"Textbook of Dialectical Materialism" translated by Li Da, Bigengtang Edition

"The Origin of the Family, Private Property, and the State" translated by Li Yingqiao, New Life Edition

"The Soviet Political and Legal System" translated by Shi Fuliang, New Life Edition

"The Peasant Problem" translated by Lu Yiyuan, Far East Edition

"Women and Society" translated by Shen Duanxian, Kaiming Edition

"New Education Outline" compiled by Ji Haowu, Nanqiang Edition

"New Education in Soviet Russia" written by Nirin, Beixin Edition

"The Foundation of Christianity" translated by Ye Qifang, Shenzhou Edition

After reading these books, you can then go on to study the actual problems of China. There are many books that should be read carefully, such as the complete works of Mr. Sun Yat-sen.

B. According to the first research order, you can read:

"Sun Yat-sen's Autobiography" in the Complete Works of Sun Yat-sen

"Adam Smith" written by Liu Binglin, Commercial Press Edition

"Ricardo" written by Liu Binglin, Commercial Press Edition

"Biography of Marx" edited by Li Wei, Shang, Middle, and Lower volumes, Shezhou Edition

"Lenin's Memoirs" Zhenwu Edition, available at all bookstores

"Lenin's Biography" International Translation and Reporting Agency

"History of the French Revolution" by Kropotkin, Upper and Lower volumes, Shenzhou Edition

"Outline of Social Problems" by Guo Zhen, Upper and Lower volumes, Shanghai Society of Social Economics Edition

"Complete History of Social Movements" Upper and Lower volumes, Pingfan Edition

"Outline of the History of Social Evolution" written by Lu Yisu, Guangming Edition

After reading all the above books, you can continue reading the books in category "A". If you start reading from category "A" first, you should also supplement with the books in category "B".

The books listed above are not carefully selected. I am just listing some for the moment, better than just opening a medical record without prescribing a prescription. A detailed book list will be included in the first volume of the Self-Study Series of this department, "How to Self-Study Social Sciences", which will be more carefully reviewed and selected. I won't go into detail here.

By mail: To Mr. Miao Wenjun: Please refer to this letter, and I will not answer your letter separately.
