Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

University Students Dancing 303

— Wen Li

The patrons of Shanghai's dance halls, besides the semi-gentlemen who are busy with social affairs, are mostly university students. Some university students even indulge in the melodies of music all night, spending money lavishly, and during the day they simply wander in a dreamlike state, and attending classes is completely irrelevant to them. On Saturday nights, dance halls are open until dawn, and it is said that some diligent students who have classes the next day still go to dance halls to dance that night. I once discussed this issue with friends, and some people advocated that university authorities should strictly prohibit university students from going to dance halls, and expel those who violate the rules. The method would be to send personnel to investigate specifically, and take action immediately upon discovery. However, some people believed that if a certain university president strictly enforced this method, it would definitely cause a disturbance, and the president would feel uneasy in their position. The best solution would be to hold tea dances on Sundays on campus, on the one hand, only allowing dancing on campus and prohibiting reckless behavior outside of campus, and on the other hand, setting a high entrance fee, at least ten yuan per ticket, just like the government's prohibition of opium, to achieve prohibition through taxation. However, some people also believed that this type of legislation would not only fail to prohibit university students from dancing, but might even educate the entire student body to dance, which would be harmful and not beneficial. The best solution would be to announce that students who want to enter dance halls to dance are not violating any rules, but should simply pay a dance prohibition fee of a certain amount each semester (it could be as high as one hundred yuan or more), which would be a legal action of achieving prohibition through taxation.

Modernized life, in Shanghai, can be considered to have been imitated to the peak, and the dancing life of university students, especially, is proof of the harm of imitating modernity. We Chinese do not imitate the content of other people's modernity, but we prefer to learn their modern appearance. This is a matter related to the future destiny of the nation, not just a trivial matter of life. Although dancing has "existed since ancient times" in China, it has long been lost. It was only after the imperialists invaded our Chinese market that dancing was brought along with them. At first, it was just the blue-eyed foreigners opening up venues and dancing themselves, but later it was learned from the upper-class Chinese, to the point that now anyone who is willing to spend three and a third cents to dance once is intoxicated and crazily modernized. (Now there are even dance halls offering a big discount of three and a third cents for two dances to attract customers.) The purpose of university students entering school is to study knowledge in order to pursue advanced studies and serve society after graduation. Now, instead of studying knowledge, they go to dance. This phenomenon is certainly enough to prove that university education has become a problem, but it can also be predicted in advance that these university students who prioritize dancing over attending classes will definitely become parasites who do not engage in production and only enjoy happiness when they reach society. People who are concerned about the world should take this as a concern!

New Year on the Road 304

— Jiong

The sky was gradually darkening, blurring, and the evening scene appeared even more like a beautiful painting. A round red sun hung obliquely in the sky, far away, bidding farewell to our eyes, reflecting a huge, piercing light; the branches stood still without swaying, like desolate maidens, harboring endless thoughts.

The clock had just struck three in the afternoon, there was no biting cold wind, and the weather felt warm; alone, in order to reduce the annoyance of being confined to this small room all day and some of the stifling atmosphere, I carelessly threw on an old, indescribable overcoat, casually got dressed, and ran out onto the road, hoping to vent the loneliness of sitting at home!

The straight road seemed to carry the desolate scene of autumn. Night was falling, and everything was shrouded in a faint, smoky coat. In a quiet mood, I quietly and silently strolled across one road and turned to another, cycling forward like this, not knowing where I would end up? I nervously pondered in my heart, constantly pondering like this.

In addition to the usual hustle and bustle of the street, the passing pedestrians seemed even more crowded! Large baskets of food and fruit were heavily hanging in everyone's hands, and some, sitting in rickshaws, had their purchases placed on the rickshaw. Ah! So it's the Lunar New Year! Strangers walking behind me cheered to each other.

The more I walked, the lighter I felt than before, using swift steps, constantly moving forward. In this quiet realm, my mind was free from worries like tangled silk threads, only feeling that in the faint, misty wisps of black smoke, everything was blurred, dim, and unclear!

The Lunar New Year has arrived again, how easily the year has passed! Hasty, muddled, I have passed another year-end. At this time, in theory, shouldn't I enthusiastically celebrate this New Year and hold a grand ceremony to commemorate it? Who would have thought that I would feel powerless and only experience the New Year on the road?

In the dim sky, there appeared layers of chasing gray clouds; after several hours of wandering, I now felt too tired to struggle forward. I stopped walking, turned around, and returned home, where it was already dusk illuminated by lights.

Young Master Writer 305

— Wang Ci

…The young master writer's surname and given name are unknown,

Because the writer's demeanor is close to that of a "young master",

So everyone calls him "Young Master Writer"…

Closing the door, he turned around in a foxtrot style, looked at the stationery on his writing desk, arranged with original manuscript paper printed with his name, Waterman ink, a Parker pen, Wasp brand cigarettes, and a glass of white milk… He thought to himself:

"Such a good environment! Let's write!"

He sat in the swivel chair, took a sip of milk, and lit a cigarette; pulled the manuscript paper straight, and picked up the pen... What should I write?

He put down the pen, and again drank milk and smoked a cigarette.

"What should I write? Write a novel? Too troublesome! No; write a poem! Yes! Writing a poem will make me a poet; "poet," such an elegant term! Miss Wang said I have a talent for writing poetry; hey! I have a talent for writing poetry."

The young master writer shrugged his shoulders, loosened his tie, and picked up the pen... It's really hard to find a subject for a poem!

The nib of the Parker pen circled a few times on the edge of the manuscript paper, but the paper remained snow-white, because the nib was held high.

"Poetry can't be separated from women: Homer, Shelley, Byron... Whose poems don't mention women?"

Again, he drank milk and smoked a cigarette.

"Yes! I have to write about women!"

So, the ink marks jumped onto the manuscript paper following the young master writer's thoughts:

Woman, my baby!

After writing it, he recited it once and felt that it had no rhythm at all, no good! A poem must have a kind of charming rhythm… Great, I have a way, it's so simple! Just add one word:

Woman!

My baby oh!

The young master writer recited it again, and a smile bloomed on his face like a flower; this "oh" word, how affectionate! No, this whole line.

Picking up the milk glass, he didn't notice that the milk was gone.

"Haha!" The young master writer seemed to suddenly realize, the vision of a great man blazed in his thoughts... There was once a great inventor Watt, no! It was probably Newton, um, perhaps not Newton either; it must have been Franklin! Um, it doesn't seem like Franklin either, never mind! In any case, he was a great inventor; didn't he once boil a watch as an egg? How is it that I didn't even know the milk glass was empty! Haha, this is a symbol, a symbol!

The young master writer was very excited, and so the poem came gushing out of his mind:

Woman oh!

I don't see you for a day!

I'm going to die in a day!

He put down the pen again, and recited it again: "The tone is really beautiful! The emotion is really intense! Of course! I have a talent for writing poetry!"

The cigarettes in the tin were gradually decreasing.

"Keep writing! I must write a full "eight lines":"

Woman oh!

I miss you,

I miss you like!

"Like what? Like "being thirsty"! No, too vulgar! Like "waiting to be fed"! Not good either! The words "waiting to be fed" are "classical Chinese", ha! Outdated "classical Chinese, get out of here"!

I miss you like a butterfly loving a flower room!

"Excellent!" The young master writer was excited to the boiling point, he thought such a line of poetry was really rare!

"One, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight, enough, this precious "eight-line poem"!"

He threw down the pen, and happiness bubbled in his heart like many bubbles; he wanted to smoke another cigarette, but there were no cigarettes left either; so, he laughed again, and thought of Watt, Newton, Franklin...

Then, let's go find country girls! 306

— Nai Shuo

My friend K, is such a funny person! At times he has a completely fresh mind, but at other times he is so pedantic as to make one nauseous. When he opens his fish-like mouth, it's rare for him to close it; but there are times when he's as silent as a cicada in winter. He loves to get close to the beautiful figures of modern ladies, but he says he already has a ten-year-old son. Below is his eulogy to his respected wife, a paean. When you think about it, you can't say he doesn't have his reasons, and the humor lies in this. Let's see:

"Now the general mentality is that new things are good, and things that aren't new are unusable. I think this is a kind of fashionable ailment. I have never opposed the old school of thought. Although new things are emerging every day, old things still have their place. Take marriage, for example. Generally, people think that non-romantic, free marriage is a sinful union. They think that in order to obtain marital happiness, one can only seek it through new-style free love, and that old-style marriage only brings pain. I think this view is very wrong. Because the old itself is not necessarily bad. It's just a matter of application. If applied properly, the old can also produce new happiness. If applied improperly, even the new will show bad signs.

I am a person who had an old-style marriage, and my marriage is the most comical farce described by the new 'Eight-Legged Essayists'. Before the marriage, I had neither seen her nor knew her temperament, let alone her thoughts. People said she was good, the matchmaker said she was good, so my parents also thought she was good and arranged it for me. Soon after the arrangement, I married her. Now I already have two children. What is most surprising is that there is still a strong affection between us, and peaceful happiness still tightly embraces us. She has never uttered a single complaint to me, and I have never felt the need to seek another home. The fact is like this, and I cannot but admit that old-style marriage also has its advantages. And the specific advantages that I feel about my wife are about the following points.

First, is her docility. General poets often praise women for being as docile as lambs, and this is only found in the wives of old-style marriages. As for new-style marriages, don't even dream about it. For example, I can ask my wife to get tea and water, I can ask her to leave me and go to another place, and I can also ask her to stay by my side all day long. What I say is always followed, and there is never any protest or resentment. In front of her, I can fully display the kind of hidden authority that is indispensable to our male dignity.

Second, is her ability to endure hardship. Endurance of hardship is a virtue, and I don't deny it at all. My wife is full of this spirit of enduring hardship. All day long, she not only tidies up the house, but also takes care of the children and washes clothes. In addition, she also has to serve my parents. If it were me, I would get very annoyed. However, she is not annoyed at all, and does not complain at all. Sometimes, even if she is so busy that her legs are weak, as long as I comfort her for a while, she will smile slightly and start working again.

Third, is her gentleness, is her thoughtfulness. This kind of taste is absolutely impossible for people who have not experienced old-style marriage to appreciate. Although the general saying is that only fashionable women understand the charms of women and know how to express the beautiful aspects of a woman's character. However, I firmly believe that only old-style wives can achieve the ultimate in gentleness and thoughtfulness. We know that if we want to appreciate a woman's expression, we often subtly understand it from her quiet gaze and lowered eyebrows. We know that a string of rambling love words is not as moving as a deep gaze. We also know that a mad embrace is not as profound as a silent closeness. The reason for this is that only from a static posture can one appreciate the true meaning of beauty, and only static beauty is the highest form of beauty. Turning to women, I think that the reason why they are able to move people more deeply is in their static beauty. And the only ones who can do this just right are old-style wives. Their silent complaints, deep gazes, and silent smiles, or silent sorrows, are truly touching and endearing.

We know that the reason we get married is to get a kind of comfort of the opposite sex's body and soul. This comfort of flesh and spirit is what people generally call marital happiness. And this kind of happiness isn't necessarily only found in new-style marriages. From my personal point of view, I feel that not only is new-style marriage not the only source of happiness, but it simply doesn't have so-called happiness. What they call love is completely based on whether there is money. If you have a full pocket, she will do her best to please you, but if the money runs out, she will be extremely vicious and then leave you.

I have always been poor, but I have never been forced to suffer by my wife, because old-style wives are better than new-style women, because there is a pure relationship between us. The old is not necessarily all bad. The new is not necessarily a good model. Not thinking like this is the root of the common people's mistakes."

He often spouts this kind of grand theory, trying to persuade his friends, and the result is that he wins everyone's agreement: "Then, let's go find country girls!" Hahaha…　　　　　　　　The End

"Welcoming the God of Wealth" 307

— Jia Wei

This thoroughly authentic "old brand domestic product" of the "New Year" has finally flowed by quickly for many days amidst the sound of gongs, drums, and firecrackers. But last night (the 17th), very strangely, the sounds of "firecrackers" and "yellow whips" with their "逼, 迫, 窮, 怕 (Bī, pò, qióng, pà; force, urgency, poverty, fear)" sounds continued non-stop all night long. It turned out that yesterday was the so-called "Day of the God of Wealth," so shop owners were enthusiastically "welcoming the God of Wealth"!

Listen! The sharp "逼, 迫 (bī, pò)" sounds of the "yellow whips," the loud "窮, 怕 (qióng, pà)" sounds of the "firecrackers," filled the whole "city night" in a soul-stirring way with the atmosphere of sulfur. Isn't this like the general shop owners, amidst the turmoil of today's world economic panic, loudly making their final, painful cries, begging to their imagined "all-powerful" "God of Wealth Bodhisattva"? And on the tables in every shop, there are all kinds of delicacies, to sincerely offer sacrifices to the "God of Wealth Bodhisattva" after he is moved by the pitiful sounds of "逼, 迫, 窮, 怕 (bī, pò, qióng, pà)" and graces them with his presence. Isn't this trying to "flatter" him with a banquet in the hope that he will bestow "wealth" upon them in abundance?

But think about it, wasn't last year's night the same? Look! Apart from the countless shops that have "closed down" in bankruptcy, there are more than 170 (?) on the most prosperous Nanjing Road in Shanghai alone that have been sued for owing more than six months' rent. So, after gorging himself on the "sincere sacrifices," what "obligations" did this "God of Wealth" fulfill?

I remember a very "humorous" dialogue in a certain novel: "Do you pray every day? Because there are too many people praying, God really has no time to listen to you." Doesn't the fact also tell us that in such a social organization, even if we piously worship this "Bodhisattva" in the store every day, what "divine power" is there to save us from avoiding this danger and "reviving the market" and "prospering Shanghai"?

Amateur Mailbox

Domestic Product Year, Factories Use Japanese Goods 308

Mr. Editor:

I am a very pitiful young worker.

You, sir, seem to be like a merciful saviour to us, and I have great faith in your amateur mailbox.

I now have a very difficult problem to solve, please give me some guidance. What is the problem? It is that the tools used in our factory have always been domestic products, but now it seems that we have sensed the benefits of January 28th [the Shanghai Incident of 1932] and purchased a large batch of Japanese goods, forcing us workers to use them. We also have very good domestic products, and during this domestic product year, we should promote domestic products and recover our rights and interests. This is the way to act for the sake of our countrymen. Moreover, the Japanese are also our enemies. If we use their goods, wouldn't we be sending them money to buy bullets to shoot us? Isn't this painful! Although I do not approve of the factory's actions, if I stop working and resist the factory, my livelihood problem cannot be solved.

You see, in this environment, under the power and oppression, what can I do to resist without working and reason with the factory? Please answer me in the newspaper as soon as possible. Wishing you good health, Cai Tuanjiu bowing. February 1st

Editor's note: This letter was received twenty days ago. When the editor first opened and read this letter, although I had endless feelings about this kind of fact, I still thought that such a frantic "factory" absolutely did not exist. However, later, after thinking about this matter again and again, and recalling the "fake domestic products" case of a certain factory mentioned in the newspaper last year, this kind of fact not only does exist, but is definitely there. If we use correct methods and calm attitudes to analyze the social phenomena of the current society, we can definitely say this.

After reading this letter, readers must be wondering: how could the "factory" be so frantic, and how could the worker be so noble? The "factory's" use of Japanese goods is nothing more than wanting to make more money, but they are people who live comfortably, and earning less money doesn't matter much. They dare to be so shameless and risk the great disapproval of the world. Workers will have no way to make a living if they lose their jobs, and they are doing things for others, and others will definitely not scold them, saying that they should not be doing Japanese goods, but he always doesn't want to, and always wants to reason with the factory. Looking at it this way, isn't there a world of difference in the personality of these two? However, that is not the case, there are other reasons for this.

All Chinese enterprises are now in the hands of imperialism. Although they sometimes want to independently resist, they ultimately cannot escape the palm of the Buddha. Because the only purpose of all enterprises in today's society is "profit." If they violate this purpose and are willing to lose money, then enterprises will not only not be able to exist, but the people who run the enterprises will definitely not have this idea. Therefore, the people who run the enterprises certainly hope that their enterprises can make money on the one hand, and can also seek welfare for the society on the other hand. However, if seeking welfare for the society cannot be achieved, or even harms the society, then as long as their enterprises can make money, they will still run them. Now the world is in economic panic, and everyone is carrying out devaluation and dumping policies. In our country, there are neither strong tariff barriers nor all kinds of unequal treaties. Think about it, how can our enterprises compete with foreigners in this environment? Therefore, it is very difficult for enterprises to exist now, that is, to make money. And doing "fake domestic product" business is not excusable, but there are other difficulties.

Therefore, it is the general working people who are exploited and oppressed by the imperialists. As for the above-mentioned entrepreneurs and comprador classes who act as accomplices or shift their suffering to the masses, on the contrary, although they are also unwilling to "rely on others to make their wedding dresses," they can still rely on the imperialists to survive, unlike the general masses who not only cannot rely on them, but are exploited and oppressed to death. Therefore, only the general hard-working masses truly have the indomitable determination to oppose imperialism.

Now let's talk about promoting domestic products. There are two reasons for promoting domestic products now: first, to break the economic chains that imperialists have placed on us, that is, "to resist foreign goods and recover our rights and interests"; second, to seek the development of national economy, thereby making society safe, in other words, to request "national wealth." At first glance, these reasons seem quite sufficient. However, practically speaking, it is already quite difficult to promote domestic products, and it is even more difficult to achieve the first two goals. We have said before that it is not easy for domestic products to compete freely with foreign products, because the sales of "domestic products" must rely on "cheap and good quality," and relying solely on patriotic enthusiasm is useless. Moreover, economic aggression is the only hope of imperialists for colonies and weak nations. Before the colonies have resistance consciousness, they put on a friendly mask and use "commercial competition" policies, but if commercial competition doesn't work, then they are straightforward and use political means to solve it, and airplanes and cannons come all at once. Therefore, imperialists always add many political chains to weak nations, such as our country's unequal treaties, because this is the guarantee of "economic aggression." Therefore, it is also useless for weak nations to use the "promoting domestic products" method to oppose imperialism.

Promoting domestic products can certainly revitalize the national economy, but what we are all praying for day and night now is social peace and prosperity, so the development of the "national economy" must also take whether or not it can achieve these goals as its future. The national economy of the United States is extremely developed, and the country is extremely rich. However, national wealth does not necessarily mean "popular prosperity" (a few "people" are extremely rich, but most people are poor). We only need to see that the United States is still craving "revival" every day, trying to make up for the economic panic, stabilize society, and reduce unemployment, and we can know that whether society is stable and whether people can live well cannot be solved by urgently seeking "wealth," and there is another way to solve it.

Therefore, if "promoting domestic products" is for the sake of seeking welfare for everyone in the society, then not only do we not dare to oppose it (those who oppose it are frantic), but it is something that everyone should pray for sincerely. However, in the current situation, judging from the reasons held by those who promote domestic products, promoting domestic products is no different from those who admired foreign ships and guns decades ago, and only knew to seek "national wealth and military strength"; their abandoning the fundamentals and pursuing the superficial is useless to society and the nation in the same way. However, although we feel that the current "promoting domestic products" is not a fundamental solution to the people's livelihood, we do not oppose it, and we hate and detest even more those "factories" who use Japanese goods like that.

What Cai Jun asked and needed was a way to "resist without doing it and reason with the factory," but the editor wrote a lot about the current "promoting domestic products," which is really irrelevant. We really have endless feelings about the occurrence of this kind of fact, and we have to say it; but we still have to talk about the solution. Now let's talk about the solution.

If you can disregard everything, then "resisting without doing it" is no problem at all, and Cai Jun doesn't need to write to this mailbox. What is the problem with resigning? However, if you think that you will have no way to make a living after resigning, and at the same time, the factory will continue to buy and use Japanese goods, then the problem is big, but it is not without a solution; this is both a solution and no solution. Because the center of this problem is whether or not the factory can be persuaded to change its mind, not to move it and make it realize its conscience. So if an individual resists without doing it, there is definitely no solution - the factory is afraid of what you will do alone, it can fire you; however, if everyone is very angry and wants to reason with the factory, then the factory may accept your and your requests because "public anger is hard to offend." Therefore, the solution that the editor can offer Cai Jun is to discuss with colleagues and ask the factory to "stop using Japanese goods."

Novel

Marriage (6) 310

— Yu Mei

"Ha, she cursed me as a prostitute. Ugh!" This surprise was slight. "People who grew up at the doorstep, who doesn't know who. She talks nonsense about me like this, am I supposed to let her? I brought out the records of her ancestors' prostitution. I said her eldest daughter slept with the big and small bosses of Wu Qiantai. Her second daughter raises illegitimate children, and the third daughter is only sixteen and already pregnant. I chewed her out thoroughly, making the old hag shrink into her turtle shell, not daring to make a sound, and that was the end of it. Ha, aren't you angry?" She looked at the man with a slight smile.

The man stuttered, "Of course. Anyone would vent such frustration."

"Of course," the third sister continued, "I don't usually like to argue with people, but she insisted on picking a fight with me, so I couldn't back down. Now she's back on good terms with me. It's really unbelievable."

"Naturally, naturally." The man lit a cigarette, pretending to listen to her with concern, while calculating something else in his heart.

After a brief pause, the woman found another topic. She asked, "Where did you go this morning?"

"This morning? I didn't go anywhere. Where did you see me?"

"At the entrance of the Anxian Lou teahouse. And there was a person in Western clothes just coming out."

"Oh, that person I nodded to? He's the third boss of Wu Qiantai, studying at Shanghai University. I just went there to mediate a labor dispute for a colleague from Wang Shunxing's company. We settled it at the teahouse."

"Wasn't Wang Shunxing's business doing well last year? Why are they laying people off?"

"Business isn't bad, but it's not great either, right? They cut a lot of people, and several of us managed to keep one person."

"Wang Shunxing's pastries are really good. Little Jade's creations are the best. I don't really like sweet things anymore."

"Didn't you used to have people sending you gifts every day?" the man said, touching the woman's face.

"Too bad you never gave me any!" The woman smiled and lightly kicked the man's leg.

"Then is it too late now?" the man teased, while still smoking.

"You're old, still saying these things." The woman pretended to be serious but smiled, glancing at the man.

"Don't act old. You look like you're eighteen." The man put his hand on the woman's leg for a long time.

While chatting and smoking, he offered the third sister a few puffs. Only when the last bit of cigarette was burned did he put down the pipe and caress the third sister for a while. He took out a dollar and placed it on the ashtray. The woman said,

"Don't leave money."

"You want me to leave that instead?" The man smiled, straightened his melon-cap hat, and walked out the door.

The woman immediately turned on the lamp on the table, grabbed it, and followed the man out the door, lighting his way outside. She put the lamp inside the doorway to shield it from the wind, and stuck her head out to say, "It's dark, muddy, and very slippery."

Film Supplement

An Overview of the Freely Developing French Film Industry 311

— Donglin

Because very few French films are imported into our country, the Chinese people do not have a correct understanding of French cinema. Therefore, here I would like to give a brief introduction to the general situation of the French film industry, which I believe will be welcomed by the readers!

First, we should know that France is a country with a very long history and a very developed sense of individual freedom. Because of its long history, many archetypes and schools have emerged in its film works; and because of the desire to express individual freedom, filmmakers also follow their individual personalities to produce all kinds of films. From this, we can know that the content of French films is diverse and cannot be generally classified as being one thing or another. For example, there may be two films that share the same fundamental concepts and emotions of French filmmaking, but everything else holds different forms and content. From this, it can be imagined that we absolutely cannot infer the entire French film industry from one or two films.

As mentioned above, in France, individuals sing their own songs of freedom, and this phenomenon can also be seen in film companies. In France, we see a state of disunity among small companies. These small companies each determine a certain goal before they start making films, rather than producing them non-stop throughout the year. Therefore, there are companies that only produce one or two films a year, and there are also companies that are founded solely for the production of one film. This proliferation of small companies, on the one hand, contributes to the production of films with new flavors that are outside the scope of large companies, but on the other hand, it also has the disadvantage of shoddy production. In short, in the French film industry, all kinds of filmmakers are acting under their own consciousness and intentions, providing the audience with films of different qualities.

Currently, the largest film company in France is (Patia Natan). This company has many excellent directors and stars, and has franchised cinemas throughout France. We can say that the company holds the reins of the French film industry.

In the last year or two, French films have rarely had original stories, and most are film adaptations of novels and plays. This tendency, on the one hand, is due to the entry of people from the theater world (such as theater actors and playwrights) into the film industry, and on the other hand, it is also because it is a relatively safe method to bring works that are already known to the world to the screen.

These kinds of films can be broadly divided into the following two types: the first is the film adaptation of ancient famous works, which can be said to be a work of art; the second is light comedies that are only meant to entertain people. In the latter, the extensive use of song and dance is a given, and France is especially rich in this kind of light-hearted, humorous work.

Film Review

The Bowery 312

— Luo Ping

The unkempt appearance, the weathered cabaret singer, the rough and barbaric hooligan, the drawn-out screams, the pervasive smoke, the chaotic jumping of a group of low-class people. This is what "The Bowery" depicts.

The United States' dispatch of troops to Cuba is a vigorous demonstration of the Monroe Doctrine. Thus, "The Bowery" uses this topic to promote the power of the sovereign state in today's turbulent Pacific situation.

Here, "The Bowery" clearly has a different meaning from the Soviet Union's "Road to Life," although they both depict hooligans and wanderers. The latter points out that wandering children should organize themselves and sacrifice themselves for the benefit of the broad masses of people and the construction of society, while "The Bowery" wants proletarian hooligans to participate in a crazy imperialist war. Building for the benefit of the broad masses of people is historical progress, while imperialist war should be opposed.

In terms of performance, director Paul Walsh has achieved great success. Not only are the static and dynamic rhythms of the entire play coordinated with each other, but the handling of the pictures is obviously very careful, intelligent, and vivid. If "The Bowery" can achieve very commendable results, indelible credit should be given to this director, which is not an exaggeration.

Kike's cheerful entrance into the crowd at the tavern, taking off his hat and cheering, powerfully contrasts the indifference and insults he receives later when he loses power.

The depiction of Kike's rudeness is carved out in small details, such as his stunning the singer and the musician, and his attacking gesture when he smells a small explosion while lighting a cigar.

The scene where a man goes to put out a fire and a woman steals the money from his pants pocket very delicately exposes the ugliness of the so-called lower class.

When Kike meets Lucy and takes her home, the child Squire dislikes Lucy and is beaten by Kike. Squire angrily takes his toys and leaves Kike's home with his second wife. The depiction of that wild child is so cute, although Jack Cooper's performance is half the reason. And the singer's dancing after getting drunk in the carriage and singing at the window simply beautifies the noisy Bowery like a hundred poems.

After Kike loses power, Kike's photo is taken down and replaced with Steve's photo; Kike sadly descends the steps, suffering the insults of the crowd; Kike lowers his head sadly and silently fiddles with his watch chain; and when Kike leaves home, placing his suitcase on the table and giving money to Lucy: Lucy declines, but Kike insists: Kike picks up the suitcase and slowly walks towards the door; Kike opens the door and painfully raises his head to look at everything in the house, until Lucy covers her face and cries, are the most astute places in the film.

In terms of dubbing, the connection with the pictures is very lively and appropriate. Such as the delicate music when Kike sees Squire sleeping in bed and when Kike and the woman kiss, such as the wildly blaring whistle when Steve falls into the water and does not get up...

A few lines in the dialogue should also be mentioned, such as Lucy saying to Steve: "You are now violating the law." And Steve replies: "The law may be wrong." Among the actors, Warner Oland is the best, Jack Cooper's meal, George Raft, Fay Wray, and the mute artist all worked very hard.

Review of "Dancing Lady" 313

— Ling He

Dancing Lady Grand Theater

Perhaps I am a very insensitive person, and after watching some movies, I often feel that there is nothing to say. This is naturally because after watching it, I have no impression of myself.

"Dancing Lady" is also the same film that will not arouse any strong interest in me. However, I don't think it's entirely because of my insensitivity, but because the film itself has no value.

Generally speaking, American films often have frivolous and superficial things, which is difficult for people who deeply feel the weight of life in the current society to have the leisure to accept this slight smile. Precisely because of this, if filmmakers closely grasp realistic themes and prick our lives, arousing our inner emotions, then we will inevitably be moved by it. Of course, this is not to ask American filmmakers to give us spiritual satisfaction, because that would be ridiculous; it is just our opinion on that kind of light and superficial work.

"Dancing Lady" is undoubtedly a frivolous work, and this is shown throughout the entire film, revealing that kind of insignificant sentiment. Like every mediocre work, it only depicts a so-called love picture of male and female entanglements. Perhaps the screenwriter wanted to add some embellishments of art for art's sake in addition to this point, like adding a few shreds of meat to a bowl of plain noodles. Originally, art for art's sake is not a fashionable thing, let alone so slight and weak here.

In short, the story here is meaningless, nothing more than commonplace and vulgar interweaving. If the lady entangled with that wealthy provincial man for her own future, showing a little of the magic of money, then how is this not extremely commonplace.

As for the song and dance scenes, they are not so amazing, and do not fully show the superficial prosperity of capitalism like "Gold Diggers of 1933". Perhaps the director also used some clever techniques in the play, such as when Joan Crawford follows Clark Gable, using the fastest tempo, which is quite interesting. And the various things in the gym are also vivid. However, it is in these places that the light style is achieved. As for the acting skills of the male and female leads, there are no special strengths.

Finally, perhaps some people will say that the level of criticism is too high, but for American films with such advanced film technology, why should we lower the level?

Wang Renmei's Kitten 315

— Qingxia

When Wild Rose Wang Renmei saw Li Lili raising a white puppy, she also went to raise a kitten. This kitten is very lively, and always cries "Meow" when it sees Wang Renmei. When Wang Renmei sees it, she also always calls "Meow." Sometimes she would hold it in her arms and say to it: "Meow! Don't make noise! I'll sing 'Peach Blossom Red' for you." Epic Film "Such Is Life" 316

Opening at the Guanglu Lanxin Theater

The latest production of Majestic Lion Films, "Such Is Life," is satirical, profound, tense, and humorous. It depicts the dreamlike nature of life and the illusion of wealth and poverty in a reasonable and well-reasoned manner. It is a masterpiece that awakens the world. The whole story tells the story of a couple and their beloved daughter who run a tea shop in England. The daughter falls in love with a young painter, but is troubled by her poor fate and cannot achieve her ambitions. Later, they receive a huge inheritance from their uncle, and they suddenly become rich, setting up a house and preparing a car, becoming a wealthy family. They hold a grand banquet for guests, singing a song that resounds through the clouds. The joy is overwhelming, and they cannot contain their happiness. The next day, unexpectedly bad news comes: the inheritance is completely divided by the bank. Yesterday's wealth is today's poverty. Fortunately, the painter becomes famous in one fell swoop, and his reputation is ten times greater. He still loves the girl, and when the two meet again, their old love reignites. The painter provides financial assistance to buy back the tea shop and revitalize their business. The old couple smile happily when they see their old home, recalling the past as if it were a dream.

Film Novel

Queen Christina (10) (3) 317

— Hu Ju

Antonio stared at her and said, "Why didn't you tell me who you were in the first place?" Christina felt that his voice had softened a lot, so she was very happy and said, "I often thank God for giving me that opportunity to travel incognito. To be able to meet you among the millions of people in the world. To you, I am not a queen, but just an ordinary woman. At that time, I was not a puppet sitting on a golden throne. But now that you have seen me in this disguise, all the beauty and joy are not cancelled out? Then why did you want to tell me my status, to hasten the rapid destruction of all beauty and joy?" Antonio sighed and said, "For you, I have committed the crime of deceiving the monarch." Christina asked, "The crime of deceiving the monarch?" Antonio said, "If someone sent a friend to woo a woman..." Christina interjected, "Joke, what love is there in your mission; it's just a clever chess piece on the European chessboard. But what we said in that snowy little inn was..."

Antonio resolutely said, "We don't need to mention everything before. Let's pretend it didn't happen." All the joy on Christina's face disappeared. She said faintly, "Alright. Then carry out your mission and try to get me to agree to your request." Antonio glared at her and said hatefully, "If I said a word that would be punished by death, I would still have to say it. You are really a royal whore. How you must laugh at my foolishness and naivety. Well, let me tell you, since I left you, I have been dreaming of you day and night, restless! Good, your victory is complete. What else do you want?" After he finished speaking, he turned around. Christina walked closer to him, raised her head and said to him, "Just this." Antonio said, "Please send me away." Christina's voice was full of enthusiasm and said, "Our love is sincere, and I believe it even more now. Why do you still go against your wishes and push me away? Can our words be changed? Can our love be changed?..."

Antonio could no longer restrain his heart. He suddenly knelt down and shouted, "Christina, my dearest." She stroked his hair. Outside, the orchestra played soft Spanish music, which was the tune played by Antonio's attendants in the inn that snowy night. Christina asked Antonio, "Antonio, do you remember?" Antonio suddenly stood up and hugged Christina, and their love was united again. But love in the royal family is not like love among ordinary people, and it is often destroyed by great forces. The biggest destructive force here is Finance Minister Magnus. He used Prince Charles and the power of the people, because the people, at the suggestion of Prime Minister Oxenstierna, had long formed a mind against the king marrying a foreigner, and especially opposed the Spanish king, because he was a Catholic monarch, while Sweden was a Protestant country. As things became more and more dangerous, Prime Minister Oxenstierna knew about Magnus and Charles' dangerous plot, but he could no longer stop it. (To be continued)
